{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2020-08-26 16:40:58","updatedTime":"2020-08-26 16:40:58","title":"5 Fashion-Girl Ways to Style Classic Sneakers This Fall ","link":"http://feeds.whowhatwear.com/~r/WhoWhatWear/~3/LFWewyduD0M/how-to-style-sneakers-for-fall","description":"<p>Styling boots and sweaters come the fall season typically feels like a piece of cake—comfortable if you will. But when it comes to styling <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/best-white-sneakers\" target=\"_blank\">sneakers</a>, especially if they are not in your usual wheelhouse, things can feel a little dicey. Here to help us navigate the coolest ways to style sneakers this fall is one of my favorite content creators, <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=CYKmnRBe6hRGATjUJ6SjmqaY4eNQ-Ko-B66DLbGwCy3rjG3x0mDuiZzOKCCvtITxjG1fRDC59PlB\" target=\"_blank\">Chloé Pierre</a>. Chloé is currently based in London, which means she has an even fresher perspective on the style scene than we would get by just looking here in the United States. </p><p>What initially caught my eye when it came to Chloé was the way she styles some of the most classic and iconic sneaker styles. From my personal experience, styling such heritage sneakers like that can feel tricky, but thanks to her expert style tips ahead, I've never felt more confident about how to approach my sneaker styling this fall. From utilizing classic pieces like shirtdresses to juxtaposing the streetwear vibe with something more elegant, Chloé proves she can really hit the nail on the head when it comes to making<a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/fall-sneaker-outfits-converse\" target=\"_blank\"> such iconic sneakers</a> look their very best. </p><p>Go on to see the five ways Chloé is encouraging us to style our sneakers this season and to shop everything you'll need to copy the looks. </p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288782/how-to-style-sneakers-for-fall-288782-1598392082105-main.1200x1600uc.gif\"><figcaption>\"Pairing a structured outfit with sneakers immediately makes the look less pretentious and more practical. src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288813/minimalist-dresses-288813-1598423517300-image.0x800uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p class=\"p1\">If you’re anything like me, you like to build out a closet of great essential basics. Yep, while a love a dramatic piece or a great trend-driven item, it’s really the foundational basics that ground my wardrobe and get the most wear. But what if I told you that this fall, one of the key basics will also be one of the biggest trends that fashion insiders will get behind? Well, that is exactly what’s about to happen with the rise of minimalist dresses. Excited? Same.</p><p class=\"p1\">On the F/W 20 runways, we saw brands like Jacquemus, <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/bottega-veneta-fall-winter-2020-review\"><span class=\"s1\">Bottega Veneta</span></a>, and Dion Lee embracing minimalism, but their designs are infused with cool details that make them feel anything but ordinary. Dresses have <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/new-york-fashion-week-fall-winter-2020\"><span class=\"s1\">cutouts carved out at the hips</span></a>, one-shoulder silhouettes with exposed backs, and ribbed fabrics in cardigan-like shapes that make them instantly covetable. Ahead, see how fashion insiders are already wearing some of the biggest minimalist dress styles we can expect for fall and shop the edit.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288813/minimalist-dresses-288813-1598411369014-main.1080x1350uc.jpg\"><figcaption>I hate to pick favorites, but the one-shoulder dress has to be one of the minimal silhouettes I'm most drawn to for fall. I think this trend will really permeate fashion in the coming months—not just with dresses but tops as well.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288813/minimalist-dresses-288813-1598411619762-main.2000x3001uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Shop the trend:</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288813/minimalist-dresses-288813-1598421228228-main.960x1450uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288813/minimalist-dresses-288813-1598411535815-main.2000x2999uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288813/minimalist-dresses-288813-1598413403587-main.1080x1349uc.jpg\"><figcaption>On the F/W 20 runways, cutouts were one of the key trends we couldn't stop talking about. eaderx/cdn73@2020_5/2020/08/26/08-41-07-352_38d599faf34dad12.webp","https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288813/minimalist-dresses-288813-1598420701583-main.800x0uc.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn26@2020_1/2020/08/26/08-41-02-004_bc97775eacd1f2e8.webp","https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288813/minimalist-dresses-288813-1598418429409-image.1080x1350uc.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn2@2020_1/2020/08/26/08-41-17-729_b476e5a2be4b896c.webp","https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288813/minimalist-dresses-288813-1598418550891-main.2000x3000uc.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn25@2020_5/2020/08/26/08-41-00-718_af863ccd5b77fbae.webp","https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288813/minimalist-dresses-288813-1598421688360-main.2000x2999uc.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn26@2020_1/2020/08/26/08-41-10-538_cb7fd5c3b9488a04.webp","https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288813/minimalist-dresses-288813-1598421605320-main.2000x3000uc.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn74@2020_3/2020/08/26/08-41-15-973_4e9f3046a0ee164d.webp","https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288813/minimalist-dresses-288813-1598419566230-main.822x985uc.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn17@2020_1/2020/08/26/08-41-17-708_afb966447d5ebc28.webp","https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288813/minimalist-dresses-288813-1598419807877-main.1391x1854uc.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn74@2020_6/2020/08/26/08-41-16-595_a6c4858e191428e5.webp","https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288813/minimalist-dresses-288813-1598419847126-main.800x0uc.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn50@2020_2/2020/08/26/08-41-13-903_b993aa32f91c067c.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/WhoWhatWear/~4/4FWtjXn_qE8":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn54@2020_2/2020/08/26/08-41-15-499_931ef5846207d4e3.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598431258976},{"createdTime":"2020-08-26 16:40:58","updatedTime":"2020-08-26 16:40:58","title":"I Was Beyond Excited When Fenty Skin Launched, so I Got Derms to Weigh In on It","link":"http://feeds.whowhatwear.com/~r/WhoWhatWear/~3/9sOgsAgtXqs/fenty-skin-review","description":"<p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288785/fenty-skin-review-288785-1598310746182-main.1200x900uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>You've probably heard the news by now that Rihanna's highly-anticipated Fenty Skin made its big debut last month. Team Who What Wear has been tapped into all the news updates ever since early rumors started swirling about more than a year ago, but it wasn't until July of this year that the brand became <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=WACROKTmo7hjguqfczXSLnaAQWOgbrGGseMPDMAcOR1qx_3sHIPC5XDRKhS886fUZppr8g\" target=\"_blank\">Instagram official</a> and started dispatching teaser after teaser. Not only did our team's Slack channel go crazy for this news, but I was personally so excited at the prospect of skincare from the queen, herself.</p><p>Now, I'm no stranger to the trend of celebrities slapping their names on skincare, makeup, and haircare lines. It happens all the time, and it's not always good. But after seeing successful launches from celebs like <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/tracee-ellis-ross-pattern-beauty-review\" target=\"_blank\">Tracee Ellis Ross</a>, <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/miranda-kerr-kora-organics-interview\" target=\"_blank\">Miranda Kerr</a>, and more, I'm not at all jaded on the topic. Not to mention that as a die-hard <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/fenty-beauty\" target=\"_blank\">Fenty Beauty</a> fan, I just knew Rihanna wouldn't bring sub-par skincare products to the table.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288785/fenty-skin-review-288785-1598391730251-product.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288785/fenty-skin-review-288785-1598391734304-product.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288785/fenty-skin-review-288785-1598391732554-product.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>You can imagine my dismay when leading up to launch day, I started seeing less-than-favorable reviews of the brand's first three priducts—<a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=Vvf3E1ymeZeuZM3QHZTzlNNbb5ldDdzFh8ebODBVjM1swlMtkrdOyDavv4752q_dxgo4zPf6Y_Ep\" target=\"_blank\">Total Cleans'r Remove It All Cleanser</a> ($25), <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=kVXcqzKZ8Rn79-11ZbhptLdeIf1Z2CG9v_IhfU4FlVu7HncbBYHbpkU6AVxMT3YAHJeKBqAqHEPp\" target=\"_blank\">Fat Water Pore-Refining Serum</a> ($28), and <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=3F5RNyHPThR7pA3BI0RPjscUQrLo4-FtB2UhH2o3fXynCtmvBj8pLJOAEFFL0r0Igf7Efltu3T7N\" target=\"_blank\">Hydra Vizor Invisible Moisturizer</a> ($35). I saw influencer after influencer calling out the ingredients, bashing the scent, and generally piling on in ways I hardly could have expected. Even though I'm always fully ready to give Rihanna the benefit of the doubt (even when it comes to the album we've all been waiting on for years....give it to us, sis!), I knew I had to get some expert advice before making any judgments. So, I flipped through my rolodex of experts and landed on two badass female derms to get their honest opinions on all things Fenty Skin.</p><p>Here to answer my burning questions are <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=V1rkoRIGYNTqvvgAycGEi4kLnc3D2d96F4U9RPSW6llXT2wE2BHVgA-FM0-iZNyyoVMiAmXziVgl6A\" target=\"_blank\">Jenny Liu</a>, MD, FAAD, board-certified dermatologist and assistant professor for the department of dermatology at University of Minnesota Medical School and <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=N3sEEgvoeNS1DNb7OFcBQVJ9tayIWB38aT8WhJ4cpa4h5boXdElyaWX3V7mOeo_hdZDSGUzD0rCMOjwS_q00\" target=\"_blank\">Sheila Farhang</a>, MD, board-certified dermatologist and founder of <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=6KQ1HBbrBfsizbKoF_DR4aODjgUrjia1V_0QrGDL5bL_hYq_JecB1F-_ovEe7bE0Aw\" target=\"_blank\">Avant Dermatology and Aesthetics</a>. Read on for their expert opinions and keep scrolling to see what our beauty editors think, too.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288785/fenty-skin-review-288785-1598312655401-main.1500x2500uc.jpg\"><figcaption>What are your thoughts on celebrities launching skincare lines? In your experience, are they well-formulated? \"I have no strong opinion, however, in my opinion, products are rarely formed with dermatologists on the team. That would be my only concern.\" — Liu. \"I don’t think there is a one-size-fits all answer. I think some celebrities really put thought into their brands and focus on ingredients, formulation, production, distribution while others shortcut for speed, profit, and mass production. People on the internet are huge critics, so celebrities have a lot of pressure to do it right. The one bad thing is skincare isn’t really regulated, so claims can be made without any research.\" — Farhang. One of the biggest criticisms of Fenty Skin so far has to do with the products having fragrance in them. Can you outline the most common dangers associated with including scent or fragrance in skin care products and any common reactions that can occur?  \"Fragrance is one of the most common culprits for allergic contact dermatitis, especially for those with sensitive skin. Eczema-like rashes can develop and often does not go away despite treatment due to the exposure. It takes only one exposure every three weeks to keep the reaction going.\" — Liu. \"Ok, people are rough on RiRi about this one. Yes, as dermatologists we generally recommend fragrance-free products, because many people (including myself) who have sensitive skin get increased irritation or rashes from products with fragrance. We usually recommend to keep it out so we are safe from skin irritation across the board. However, not everyone’s skin is sensitive to fragrance. Overall, I think fragrance just limits the number of people who can use it. I think it would be smart of [Rihanna] to create an extension of her line for those with sensitive skin.\" — Farhang</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288785/fenty-skin-review-288785-1598389956342-image.1200x1365uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Another big criticism is that the Fat Water Toner Serum contains witch hazel as an ingredient. What are the risks associated with including witch hazel in a skincare product? What are the benefits? \"Witch Hazel is a common ingredient found in astringents and toners. It can cause burning, contact dermatitis, redness, and irritation of the skin. It does have anti-inflammatory effects which may be helpful in treating bites, stings, and acne.\" — Liu. \"I actually don’t recommend toners to my patients unless they have super oily skin. Witch hazel is from a plant, is an antioxidant, and is used for its drying and pore-shrinking effects. The other ingredients help soothe and improve the skin barrier that may have been disrupted by witch hazel. I love that she used niacinamide in her line! It's one of my favorite ingredients to improve the skin's moisture barrier, tone, and texture.\" — Farhang. Which skin types are most susceptible to irritation from fragrances in skincare? From witch hazel?  \"I personally do not like highly scented products, and definitely do not recommend to those with sensitive and eczema-prone skin or those who have a known history of contact dermatitis.\" — Liu. \"Those with sensitive skin or eczema [are most susceptible to irritation from] fragrances. Those with dry or sensitive skin for witch hazel.\" — Farhang. If a client came into your office and told you they were using this skincare line, would you sign off on that choice? Why or why not? \"I haven't tried myself so cannot say for sure, but I'm not a big fan of fragranced products. I also evaluate all products based on research, so I would need to look at that first if it even exists.\" — Liu. \"Again, if someone doesn’t really have problematic skin—no acne, no drying, no sensitivity—then I’d say it’s fine. But it’s not all inclusive. Skincare requires fine-tuning based on the persons needs and concerns.\" — Farhang</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288785/fenty-skin-review-288785-1598391061733-main.1200x1365uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288785/fenty-skin-review-288785-1598389952541-image.1200x1365uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288785/fenty-skin-review-288785-1598391784019-product.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Rating: 5/5 stars. Cleansing is my favorite part of my skincare routine, so I can be picky about the washes I use on my face. I'm a religious double-cleanser, so I was also skeptical that this wash would be able to perform as both a makeup remover and a cleanser, as promised. To my surprise, it totally does double-duty to remove everything from stubborn eye makeup down to dirt and debris. And even better, it's not overly oily to the point that it leaves behind a residue on the skin. I like my face to feel nice and clean, but not stripped, after cleansing, and this rich wash definitely imparts that feeling. The scent is also mild and more enjoyable than your run-of-the-mill soapy cleanser smell.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288785/fenty-skin-review-288785-1598391783039-product.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Rating: 4/5 stars. I saw an influencer say that she wouldn't even put this product on her face, citing the use of witch hazel, dye, and fragrance in the ingredient list as red flags. I have to admit that I approached this one with some trepidation. I grew up in a generation where straight witch hazel was the go-to toner of all the pre-teens in my class, so the use of it here didn't really scare me. I was more concerned about pressing dye and unknown fragrance ingredients into my skin and risking irritation. So far, I've not experienced any adverse reactions to this product! I will say that I'm still a bit hung up on the combination of toner and serum, as those two products tend to have very different goals, so I'm still trying to wrap my mind around that part of it. But as far as ingredients go, I'm happy to see nourishing additions like niacinamide, aloe, and hyaluronic acid high on the list.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288785/fenty-skin-review-288785-1598391781929-product.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Rating: 5/5 stars. Rihanna and her makeup artist have said on the record many times that she has oily skin, so I really wasn't expecting this moisturizer to be able to keep up with the dry zones of my combination skin. Like other lightweight moisturizers, I expected it to only be able to provide hydration for an hour or two before being swallowed up my the area around my mouth, which tends to become parched throughout the day. That hasn't happened yet, and I'm so pleased about it! I knew I could count on my girl Rihanna to deliver an SPF moisturizer that would be completely transparent on my brown skin, and she didn't let me down there. I've only worn this moisturizer indoors and under minimal makeup so far, but based on the texture and how it performs over the course of the day sitting in from of the computer under intense (sometimes drying) air-conditioning in my house, I'm inclined to believe that it would hold up well outside, too. In terms of the scent, I was already a fan of the Fenty Beauty Pro Filt'r Instant Retouch Primer ($32) which smells exactly like this moisturizer, so it didn't bother me. The fragrance is pretty sweet and it lingers, so I can totally understand the criticism there. Even though I'm more into unscented skincare nowadays, the scent here is not a deal-breaker for me. Plus, the refillable packaging is absolutely genius and I love how it closes securely. That's the kind of innovation I love to see!</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288785/fenty-skin-review-288785-1598389950806-image.1200x1365uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288785/fenty-skin-review-288785-1598389954593-image.1200x1365uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288785/fenty-skin-review-288785-1598389917621-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Rating: 5/5 stars. Despite all of the buzz and hubbub surrounding the Fenty Skin launch, I tried to go into my personal trial with zero expectations or bias. And, honestly, I've been super impressed. Overall, the line exceeded my expectations, and this cleanser, in particular, ticks every single box for me. A little goes a long way—literally, you only need a pea-sized amount—which makes the $25 price tag more feasible if you're used to a face wash that's less of a splurge. That said, you definitely get your money's worth with this cleanser. It feels so soft and silky on your face as you lather and massage it into your skin. I almost want to say it's pillow-like? It truly does remove every last trace of makeup or dirt from your face, but unlike so many cleansers on the market, this leaves your skin feeling plush, energized, and healthy afterward. There's also no residue or stickiness—truly, nothing gets my goat more than when you wash your face and there is some kind of film left behind that makes you feel like you have to re-wash all over again. Now, I know this line received lots of backlash due to the scent, but personally, I take zero issue with the fragrance. RiRi is known for her love of sweet, intoxicating perfumes, so the fact that her products have a touch of sweet fragrance feels pretty on-brand for her. I don't find it overly-saccharine, and I actually have really come to enjoy it. The way I see it, if you're looking for a really clinical or medicinal skincare regimen devoid of personal touches like fragrance, you're probably not going to be buying from a line like this anyway. My one and only concern with this cleanser is it contains a few coconut-derived surfactacts (which are often found in clean, or more natural skincare formulations) that have, historically, broken me out. I haven't had any issues with this cleanser in that regard thus far, so I'm keeping my fingers crossed. I would love to continue using this in my day-to-day skincare routine.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288785/fenty-skin-review-288785-1598389922522-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Rating: 5/5 stars. This is a really interesting product, and honestly, I wish I had something critical to say about it to make this review more interesting, but I don't! I'm actually not much of a toner girl, but I do love serums containing hydrating, plumping, and brightening ingredients. This toner-serum hybrid has most of my faves like aloe, hyaluronic acid, and niacinamide, plus a few extras like Kahlahari melon, witch hazel, and baobab. I also love that you can apply it with your hands (the consistency is more viscous, like a typical HA serum so it doesn't run all over the place), and you're not wasting cotton pads. I would say the only way I feel like this product resembles a toner is that it does, in fact, reduce shine and minimize the look of your pores. It does everything the marketing tells you it will, so again, I take zero issue with it!</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288785/fenty-skin-review-288785-1598389948146-image.1200x1365uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288785/fenty-skin-review-288785-1598389926516-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Rating: 5/5 stars. Plot twist—I am obsessed with this moisturizer-SPF hybrid. OBSESSED. It makes my skin look pore-less, glass-like, smooth, and radiant, and it's positively dreamy underneath makeup. So many moisturizers with sunscreen feel really heavy and tacky on my skin, and I almost always end up with pimples and congestion after just a few days of wearing them regularly. But not this one! I love the re-fill feature with this (it feels so much less wasteful!), and I'm really into the packaging and sleek pump design, in general. Even better, the formula truly does keep oil and grease at bay all day damn day. You retain the luminous, airbrushed-esque finish the entire time your wearing it without any extra shine encroaching by 5 pm. I've never had a moisturizer or SPF look exactly the same on my face at both 7 am and 7 pm. I mean, have you?!  If you only buy one product from Fenty Skin, this would be my top recommendation.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img 16:40:58","updatedTime":"2020-08-26 16:40:58","title":"Buying Black Is a Forever Mood—Here Are 30 Beauty Items Worth Ringing Up Now","link":"http://feeds.whowhatwear.com/~r/WhoWhatWear/~3/YtKCYtlVgJY/black-owned-beauty-brands-sephora-ulta-nordstrom","description":"<p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288777/black-owned-beauty-brands-sephora-ulta-nordstrom-288777-1598372465850-main.1200x900uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>Twenty-twenty has been a year of learning, to say the least. Of all the lessons brought to the forefront, the systemic injustices faced daily by Black people in this country have been among the most prominent. The conversations surrounding this topic have been eye-opening for many, and, at times, extremely uncomfortable for all, but one silver-lining has been the widespread resolution to help close the gap by amplifying and supporting <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/black-owned-beauty-brands\" target=\"_blank\">Black-owned businesses</a>. This step won't solve every issue facing the Black community, but it's certainly a step in the right direction.</p><p>As the social media outrage and the public displays start to quiet down, it's important to remember that combatting performative allyship means continuing to do the work, like supporting Black-owned businesses, even after the hashtags have settled. And while buying Black may take a little extra thought, you may be surprised to find that it doesn't even have to mean visiting retailers you don't already frequent. (Although, there are plenty of <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/black-owned-beauty-retailers\" target=\"_blank\">up-and-coming retailers</a> dedicated to this cause that fully deserve our support, too.) Organizations like <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=60grIPYk86A4baZjb6MTMpsHURMwVPHDIsd8DwXoO_FW8NL1Kou54B8eMAIwYNWjn2NdIYCb1dF7wZfz2DQzPg\" target=\"_blank\">the 15 Percent Pledge</a> have emerged to challenge and hold our favorite retailers accountable to dedicating 15% of their shelf-space to supporting Black-owned businesses, so we hope to see more of them committing to large-scale change.</p><p>Ahead, check out 30 of our favorite Black-owned beauty brands you can shop at Ulta, Sephora (it's taken <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=wQLFJ5V7WRw7yt5tuJmeEmLzaE28i3nMTj2TNGfy5_JrHRQlFbjJ1xXPmrqxxMm1TyxC-4gw\" target=\"_blank\">the Pledge</a>!), and Nordstrom via its curated beauty pop-in. Let's vote with our dollars and continue to show these corporations that we support Black-owned beauty businesses and that we expect them to continue to do so as well.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288777/black-owned-beauty-brands-sephora-ulta-nordstrom-288777-1598307463389-main.928x800uc.jpg\"><figcaption>The streets have been steadily chattering about Tracee Ellis Ross's Pattern Beauty ever since it launched last year. In addition to the initial collection of shampoos and conditioners, the brand's most recent extensions include styling products and these chic hair tools.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288777/black-owned-beauty-brands-sephora-ulta-nordstrom-288777-1598318216494-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Best known for its inclusive range of foundation shades and vibrantly-hued eye shadow palettes made to show up on even the deepest skin tones, Uoma is all about celebrating individuality and doing away with the singular and often alienating idea of what beauty should look like. This new eyebrow pencil is another winner, offering precise, hair-like strokes to enhance every brow shape. You may also recognize the brand's founder, Sharon Chuter, as the outspoken voice behind Pull Up or Shut Up, an online platform dedicated to, \"Fighting for economic opportunities for Black people,\" as explained in its Instagram bio.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288777/black-owned-beauty-brands-sephora-ulta-nordstrom-288777-1598318418242-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>This botanical haircare line ditches silicones, parabens, mineral oil, and other unhealthy ingredients and focuses instead on clean, plant-based alternatives for your healthiest curls ever. This minty wash purifies the hair and scalp with rhassoul clay and bentonite clay for a deep, non-stripping clean. </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288777/black-owned-beauty-brands-sephora-ulta-nordstrom-288777-1598318427162-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Juvia's Place has become famous for its affordable and highly pigmented eye shadow palettes, but its other offerings, including this foundation, are worth a second look, too.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288777/black-owned-beauty-brands-sephora-ulta-nordstrom-288777-1598307772360-main.0x800uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Even though some of its products are modeled after the decadent treats and ingredients you'd find in a real bakery, you can count on Beauty Bakerie's (non-edible) makeup selection to be vegan and cruelty-free. One of the most beloved products is this HD setting powder, which can be used alone or atop your favorite foundation.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288777/black-owned-beauty-brands-sephora-ulta-nordstrom-288777-1598318434045-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>This haircare line focuses on natural remedies for all your hair woes. From Hatian black castor oil formulas to this petrolerum-free scalp treatment, the brand offers everything you need to maintain healthy, shiny hair.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288777/black-owned-beauty-brands-sephora-ulta-nordstrom-288777-1598318440725-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Mixed Chicks has been holding it down for the curly community long before it became trendy to do so. Wearing","link":"http://feeds.whowhatwear.com/~r/WhoWhatWear/~3/uUP_j1mgnx0/comfortable-fall-denim-trends","description":"<p>Call me crazy but I actually miss wearing <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/new-levis-jeans\" target=\"_blank\">jeans</a>. Obviously it's been ridiculously hot as of late, but I also am just tired of feeling like I'm constantly enveloped in jersey knit. I long for something crisper and a little more dressed up, yet still familiar. That's why I've decided not to abandon <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/fall-wide-leg-jeans-outfits\" target=\"_blank\">denim</a> again as I did back in March when lockdowns began. But for fall 2020, I'm definitely buying fewer rigid, straight-leg styles and more loose, relaxed, stretchy styles.</p><p>Given the aforementioned limitations I'm placing on my denim shopping this fall, I've narrowed the options way down, to four specific styles, all of which are considerably more <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/comfortable-fall-fashion-trends\" target=\"_blank\">comfortable</a> than many jeans on the market. And after narrowing them down, I noticed something fun: Each style corresponds with the major denim trend that a past decade is known for. </p><p>So with that, scroll to shop fall's four most comfortable denim trends, that originally date back to the '70s, '80s, '90s, and '00s. </p><p>Ripped jeans are one of the most surprising trends to return this year, but based on how many celebrities and influencers are wearing them, it can't be ignored. I, for one, haven't worn distressed denim much since the 2000s, but I'm very tempted to purchase a pair. This time around, go for more subtle distressing and a slouchy silhouette (as opposed to skinny jeans).</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383554925-image.1200x1500uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383595174-product.850x850uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383603844-product.850x850uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383602355-product.850x850uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383622906-product.850x850uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383624292-product.850x850uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383649716-product.850x850uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383623797-product.850x850uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>Skater jeans is a fun trend that coincides with the overarching <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/grunge-trend-fall-2020\" target=\"_blank\">grunge theme</a> on the F/W 20 runways. This long and baggy style is comfortable for obvious reasons, and actually looks even cooler with similarly baggy pieces, so feel free to embraced the all oversized everything look when wearing them.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383556767-image.1200x1499uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383603355-product.850x850uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383600570-product.850x850uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383628784-product.850x850uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598391527316-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383630060-product.850x850uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598392017065-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>Think of pleated jeans as mom jeans 2.0. Featuring a high waist and often a tapered leg, pleated jeans are surprisingly flattering and easy to wear, in addition to being nice and roomy (AKA comfortable). </p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383558151-image.1200x1500uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383627993-product.850x850uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383575685-product.850x850uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383647262-product.850x850uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383649352-product.850x850uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383626311-product.850x850uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383637224-product.850x850uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>As is the case every few years in fashion, the '70s are back. And the return of the '70s couldn't be possible without the adjacent return of flared jeans. My best advice for making it work? Opt for a high-waisted style and wear heels (even just a low heel is better than flats with flares). Last but not least, definitely choose a pair with even just a hint of stretch to keep things comfortable.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288802/comfortable-fall-denim-trends-288802-1598383544691-image.1200x1497uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img Lately","link":"http://feeds.whowhatwear.com/~r/WhoWhatWear/~3/-mRjAtr9QRQ/short-bob-hairstyles","description":"<p>It's not news that 2020 has been a <em>very</em> different kind of year for many different reasons. Alas, despite the socially-restricted parameters the world has faced for months, there has not (surprisingly) been any shortage of <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/celebrity-new-haircut\" target=\"_blank\">amazing celebrity hair inspiration</a>. Salons may have been (or are still) closed for the better part of 2020, but our favorite members of the A-list have proven to be ultra-resilient on the cool hair front.</p><p>One style, in particular, that's continued to burn brightly are <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/shoulder-length-hairstyles\" target=\"_blank\">bobs and lobs</a>, and for the past few years and into 2020, celebrities have been shedding their extensions or natural length in favor of chic bob hairstyles that are short, long, and anywhere in between. To take <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/low-maintenance-haircuts\" target=\"_blank\">the popular haircut trend</a> even further, they've been adding detailed accents like headbands, clips, and braids aplenty in addition to <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/fall-hair-colors\" target=\"_blank\">pops of unexpected color</a>. (From platinum blonde to baby pink.) Ahead, we're sharing 20 short bob hairstyles our favorite celebrities have been endorsing recently and which, we have a feeling, might just inspire you to try the cut out yourself. (Once it's safe to see your styling professional again, that is.) panties</a>\" are really just a funny term that refers to briefs or high-rise underwear. The stereotype that your grandmother only wears a certain style of underwear has officially been squashed but due to the booming acceptance of fashion having no age limit, women of all ages have been rocking the \"granny panty\" for years now, and to be honest, I personally find them very sexy.</p><p>Since everyone has been spending much more time indoors these days, the sartorial Instagram content flooding our feeds has drastically changed. What was once a sea of fashion girls posting the latest trends and innovative outfits have now transformed into an oasis for loungewear styling tips. One of the at-home outfits I have taken a particular interest in is a simple one, requiring only two items: <strong>a tank top and granny panties</strong>.</p><p>While sweatpants and leggings are certainly dominating the WFH scene, this new lingerie outfit is giving them a run for their money. So far, this outfit has proven it is perfect for everything from lounging around to reading a book. The best part? src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288773/shani-darden-favorite-beauty-products-288773-1598376364693-main.1200x1500uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><strong><em>The Lineup</em><em><span> is a monthly series in which we give you an inside peek at the beauty lineups of cool fashion people, editors, makeup artists, hairstylists, and estheticians—all the people we trust the most. Here's a behind-the-scenes look at all the can’t-live-without products that make their worlds go 'round.</span></em></strong></p><p>Some people grow up knowing exactly what they want to be. Some people <em>think</em> they know what they want to be until they later realize what their true passion is. <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=55pyBTNWouAX8ZaIQZqFipbLdwIxFeCc1i_vMLZU4G0vXiSjC92Grpt3MQ\" target=\"_blank\">Shani Darden</a>—one of L.A.'s most sought-after estheticians—is one of the latter: She moved from New York to L.A. to be a model when she was a teenager, but after graduating from college and taking a job at a dermatologist's office, she quickly realized that skincare was her true calling—and it's a good thing she did.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288773/shani-darden-favorite-beauty-products-288773-1598375051881-main.1200x1500uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>Now Darden has an <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=9vTQ6vSJ0XDT_HK47DEgGFy4d8ptx7ECWnQoametThgz7_C5ucEkbkH6bayQAIDcBiY5eeJ2njJ9\" target=\"_blank\">eponymous skincare line</a> and is the secret force behind stars like Rosie Huntington-Whiteley, Jessica Alba, and Chrissy Teigen's celestial complexions. <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/clean-beauty-products-for-mature-skin\" target=\"_blank\">They all have really, <em>really</em> good skin</a>—just look at any pictures of them—so you would think Darden has concocted some over-the-top skincare regimen for each, but surprisingly, she approaches each of her clients' skin the same way she does her own: a less-is-more mentality. \"I think one of the biggest myths is that you need to use a ton of products to achieve great skin. It’s really not about using the most products but about using the <em>right</em> products for <em>your </em>skin specifically,\" says Darden, who struggled with acne as a teenager. \"If you have a powerful treatment product that uses really effective ingredients and pair it with staples like a great cleanser and moisturizer, it can truly transform your skin,\" she explains.</p><p>We're always looking for ways to transform our skin, so we asked Darden to share her lineup of products and tips that have never failed her. From a retinol serum (FYI everyone should use one, according to Darden) to <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/best-sunscreens-for-dark-skin\" target=\"_blank\">staying out of the sun</a> (and protecting your skin when you're in it), these are the 18 products Darden always has on hand.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288773/shani-darden-favorite-beauty-products-288773-1598375068751-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>\"This is the treatment product I use almost every single night. Retinol Reform combines lactic acid and retinol to speed up cellular turnover to bring fresh skin to the surface, as well as boost collagen, minimize fine lines and wrinkles, reduce hyperpigmentation, and help keep skin clear. The best part is that it’s not going to cause dryness or flaking. This is the number one product I recommend to my clients to keep their skin glowing in-between facials!\"</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288773/shani-darden-favorite-beauty-products-288773-1598375074793-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>\"I love a gentle yet effective cleanser that doesn’t strip the skin. My Cleansing Serum has hyaluronic acid, which draws moisture to the skin and helps it hold onto it, along with oat-bran extract, which helps repair the skin’s barrier. I use this morning and night, and my favorite way to cleanse is to use two pieces of wet cotton gauze. It helps to gently exfoliate and make sure all traces of the cleanser are removed.\"</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288773/shani-darden-favorite-beauty-products-288773-1598375081094-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>\"Finding a great moisturizer that works well for your skin type is so important. For more normal-to-oily skin like mine, I prefer a lightweight oil-free moisturizer like my namesake one, which is formulated with hyaluronic acid to deeply hydrate the skin without causing any congestion. It also has hydrolyzed collagen, which helps to keep the skin smooth and supple.\"</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288773/shani-darden-favorite-beauty-products-288773-1598375086891-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>\"I use this every morning before sunscreen for antioxidant protection. This vitamin C serum helps to offset the effects of environmental stressors like pollution and UV exposure. It’s powerful yet still very nourishing for the skin.\"</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288773/shani-darden-favorite-beauty-products-288773-1598375093815-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>\"A hyaluronic acid serum is always a staple for me in the morning before sunscreen and at night before moisturizer. 16:40:58","updatedTime":"2020-08-26 16:40:58","title":"What Is Polyester Made Of?","link":"http://feeds.whowhatwear.com/~r/WhoWhatWear/~3/rkw9A307KRs/what-is-polyester","description":"<p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/244695/what-is-polyester-244695-1597187575004-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>While the first thing that comes to mind at the mention of polyester might be retro bowling shirts and vintage floral dresses, this ubiquitous fabric is probably in more of your wardrobe than you think. From athletic-wear to lingerie, polyester can be found in an array of everyday attire. As apparel made from cotton and other natural materials has decreased, the use of polyester in clothing manufacturing has become more popular than ever. But what is polyester, exactly? Read on to learn what polyester is, where can it be found, and what you need to know about this popular fabric.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/244695/what-is-polyester-244695-1597187637621-main.1200x1598uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><span>Simply stated, <strong>polyester is a synthetic fabric comprised of a type of plastic</strong>. Less simply stated, polyester is <strong>made up of molecular polymers</strong> <strong>associated with the </strong></span><strong><a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=YIhoGqW_9Y6gn5sqzI2KpOoh9TKxIBWaAuczSmj02NpRkvs3F79P1KCU6zCw1IMmjuzf\">ester</a></strong><span><strong> group of chemical compounds</strong> (hence the term “polyester”). While there are many variations of polyester, a common one is \"polyethylene terephthalate,\" or PET, a type of plastic found in clothing and packaging. Liquid polyester is stretched and spun into fabric using an industrial <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=Uxszp-tsws9UHT2I8ENWgESy-4f23pl0HXnLZ1Ih7UnzJLi5BQsBI9u1BXi_cUFwN5ECs56kW3fQUsKazswiFstS\" target=\"_blank\">spinneret machine</a>.</span></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/244695/what-is-polyester-244695-1597187662013-main.1200x1598uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><span>One of the most common questions surrounding what polyester is has to do with where it can be found. Following its invention in the early 1940s and its </span><a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=wQE31bE1iW8oZFWqwIOPNA6ZJLyweoQt4LydsWNlxbdXXcvHBRGJLEey29AP_ta3fy1F81pnmlcQR3a_Ng\"><span>introduction to the public in 1951</span></a><span>, polyester would go on to dominate decades’ worth of yearbook photos in the form of lightweight jackets, leisure suits, and brightly colored A-line dresses. </span></p><p><span>Today, polyester can still be found in dresses, blouses, and slacks, though most often in conjunction with other fabrics like cotton, wool, and nylon. Because of its remarkable versatility (and relatively low-maintenance care instructions), polyester is also found in a wide array of outerwear, athleisure, and fitness apparel.</span></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/244695/what-is-polyester-244695-1597187673163-main.1200x1598uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><span>There are a number of reasons that polyester has gained such widespread appeal. It’s <strong>highly wrinkle-resistant</strong>, making it an attractive choice for activewear and travel attire. It’s also <strong>moisture-resistant and flexible</strong>, which makes it a popular choice among many athletes. </span></p><p><span>On the other hand, </span><a href=\"http://www.whowhatwear.com/worst-fabrics-for-skin\"><span>research has shown</span></a><span> that polyester may not be the best fabric for those with sensitive skin, especially since it’s not particularly breathable. It’s also not ideal for those who prefer clothing made from natural, biodegradable materials. If you’re not sure which of your clothing contains polyester, the best education on polyester may be found by taking a look through your wardrobe.</span></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/244695/what-is-polyester-244695-1598393732458-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/244695/what-is-polyester-244695-1597188339786-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/244695/what-is-polyester-244695-1597188706675-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/244695/what-is-polyester-244695-1597188890734-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/244695/what-is-polyester-244695-1598394947981-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/244695/what-is-polyester-244695-1597188979354-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img In fact, we recently highlighted the <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/casual-fall-dresses\" target=\"_blank\">casual fall dresses we have our eyes on at the moment</a>. Next, we thought we’d focus on one of the hardest-working sections in our closets: <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/basics-styling\" target=\"_blank\">our basics</a>. These simple items—like neutral tees and classic knits—act as the foundational elements in our wardrobes in that they can easily be mixed and matched with some of our other trendier items to create those well-balanced, forward looks. On that note, there are actually a few basics that we’d consider to be the handiest items in each of our specific wardrobes.</p><p>The items in question are basics that we routinely wear on repeat and would essentially never give up thanks to their versatile nature. src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287143/podiatrist-approved-house-shoes-287143-1589115548912-main.0x800uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>Your <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/most-comfortable-shoe-trends\" target=\"_blank\">shoe choice</a> more or less determines how comfortable you’ll remain throughout the day. Regardless of how cozy your clothing selection is, if your pair of flats or sandals pinch ever so slightly, your comfort level will swiftly start to decline. In an effort to avoid such discomfort, we often tap podiatrists to shed insight on those <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/best-womens-shoes-for-feet\" target=\"_blank\">current footwear silhouettes that won’t cause as much pain</a>.</p><p>Today, given that many are spending more time at home, we wanted to zero in on the best (and worst) shoes to wear around the house. We turned to <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=XE4GsYrkEHOarF5cduD7f-neF83-REjA1wl7IBZpbUQtMOUf0fCUeEMaAu_ENL4KgBiuRdutdg\" target=\"_blank\">Benjamin Tehrani</a>, DPM, of <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=DxkDLy4-xlt7IUvceowuUd2c33TpBzxpXd4-cKblhPScPDQiXF-GPeJbNRLA3avjtljNag\" target=\"_blank\">Kings Point Foot & Ankle</a> in Los Angeles for expert tips on the common styles that are okay and those that could cause some harm to your overall foot health. In addition, given that many of us do spend a lot of time walking barefoot around the house, Tehrani shed light on the pros and cons on that front, too.</p><p>Without further ado, keep scrolling for a ranking of the best and worst at-home shoes. And if you’re shopping at the moment, you’ll find shoe recommendations that could be of interest as well.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287143/podiatrist-approved-house-shoes-287143-1589115526084-main.1080x1350uc.jpg\"><figcaption>\"Supportive sandals are preferred. I am impressed with styles like those from Birkenstock that have the ability to remain in style while also providing the best support in the arches that I've seen to date. They have a soft foot bed that has an integrated latex foam cushion that molds to your feet the more you walk in them. The insole is leather lined so it helps to keep the feet dry and makes it durable, which is why they're typically more expensive than the typical sandal.\" — Tehrani</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287143/podiatrist-approved-house-shoes-287143-1588861205744-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287143/podiatrist-approved-house-shoes-287143-1588861486034-product.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287143/podiatrist-approved-house-shoes-287143-1588861278200-main.3320x3566uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287143/podiatrist-approved-house-shoes-287143-1588861404635-product.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287143/podiatrist-approved-house-shoes-287143-1588861825701-main.1128x2000uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287143/podiatrist-approved-house-shoes-287143-1588860320372-image.1080x1248uc.jpg\"><figcaption>\"I prefer to wear a supportive sandal or slipper versus walking barefooted. Our bodies have adapted to the new-world environment of this concrete jungle, and our feet could use the support more than ever. There is absolutely nothing wrong with walking barefooted around the house but in moderation. For instance, if I am washing dishes or doing my laundry, I know I'll be spending lots of time standing in one place and putting pressure on my heels, arches, and balls of my feet. Even if you're in excellent shape, spending hours on your feet without support can lead to many foot, knee, and hip soft-tissue impairments! In those instances where I know I'm going to be on my feet for more than a half-hour, I prefer to wear sandals, such as Powersteps or Vionic, which have built-in orthotics that support your arches. \"If you're going the sock route, cotton socks help wick sweat away, for those of you whose feet sweat a lot. Cotton is also thicker and provides more comfort for your feet, especially for people who can't stand wearing sandals or slippers around the house.\" — Tehrani</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287143/podiatrist-approved-house-shoes-287143-1588861991993-product.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287143/podiatrist-approved-house-shoes-287143-1588862546809-product.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287143/podiatrist-approved-house-shoes-287143-1588862765440-product.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287143/podiatrist-approved-house-shoes-287143-1588862833759-main.3320x5092uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287143/podiatrist-approved-house-shoes-287143-1588860321302-image.1080x1167uc.jpg\"><figcaption>\"Pay attention to the bottom sole of the sandal or flip-flop. As a general rule of thumb, if it bends in the middle of the sole, it has very poor support and your feet will tire out quickly. Take your thumb and middle finger and grab the heel, do the same thing with your other hand on the ball of the sandal, then squeeze. If the central portion bends, it's literally doing nothing to support your arches during your walking cycle.\" — Tehrani</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img 16:40:58","updatedTime":"2020-08-26 16:40:58","title":"This Sunscreen Mistake Is Easy to Make—Here's How to Fix It","link":"http://feeds.whowhatwear.com/~r/WhoWhatWear/~3/VoINkNAYlfM/best-sunscreens-for-rosacea","description":"<p>By now, we know that <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/best-body-sunscreens\" target=\"_blank\">wearing sunscreen</a> every day is so important. Protecting your skin against damaging UV rays is crucial to reducing your risk of developing <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/suncare-skin-routine\" target=\"_blank\">skin cancer.</a> Plus, it will stop your skin from aging faster. Yep, sun exposure can really speed up the process. According to the <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=cZaBpt2SMpB2aVJzQxA0-SncRQ5YiSijXomU0_mSftekttf3DnDWjwoLZIOcKIiLcZ4xiVFNiNiPUyN0YDIndHbEsbLWh2XyGr5X-l6fqf5iTG0o1n5Jregnbl-BEE6kttYmBoFZjOLEDzHxyA3RMsBt45HTxA\" target=\"_blank\">American Academy of Dermatology</a>, sun damage over time can <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/beauty-routine-for-sun-damange\" target=\"_blank\">lead to changes</a> like wrinkles, age spots, loose skin, spider veins, and a blotchy or ruddy complexion.</p><p>And while there are a lot of variables that come with choosing a sunscreen—chemical or <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/mineral-sunscreens\" target=\"_blank\">mineral</a>, SPF levels, different types of formulas—the general rule of thumb is pretty easy to remember. \"Making sure that your sunscreen product is broad-spectrum and of an SPF of at least 30 is the most important,\" says <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=UUnOMxy0GWJrr1YeXQIYwWSNqm3PZBqU26Dv5wtWTpRU-X4YxsK0CIKs5Ve36f2Jh5AQYhFSvuOSSkMvFZRf_9BdBBuc_reJEhhf\" target=\"_blank\">Joel Cohen, MD</a>, a board-certified dermatologist and director of AboutSkin Dermatology in Denver, Colorado.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288001/best-sunscreens-for-rosacea-288001-1593545586576-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>So we're all in agreement that sunscreen is a crucial <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/natural-skincare-routine\" target=\"_blank\">skincare step</a>. But we're also all human, and sometimes you might forget to apply it. Or you might skip over some body parts when you're in a rush. I like to consider myself pretty diligent about applying sunscreen every day, but I recently spent a day by the pool and thought I had gotten every nook and cranny of my body, only to find my shoulders sunburned at the end of the day. It happened five days ago, and I'm still feeling much guilt about it.</p><p><strong>One mistake that can lead us to forget? It might be that you don't have a sunscreen that you're comfortable wearing, that's easy to use, or that works with your skin.</strong> Making sure you have a sunscreen that you <em>actually</em> like wearing makes a big difference—and that comes down to personal preference sometimes. \"Many people find it easier to have a product that contains their daily moisturizer as well, as that removes one additional step from their morning regimen,\" Cohen says. \"Conversely, many people with oily skin want a product that does not add emollience or moisture to their skin. Cosmetic elegance is critically important, as patients will not use their SPF every morning if it is thick or uncomfortable on the skin.\"</p><p>This can be especially true if you have a skin condition that might make things irritated or uncomfortable, like eczema, <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/best-sunscreens-for-oily-skin\" target=\"_blank\">acne-prone skin</a>, or rosacea. If you have a sunscreen product that annoys your skin even more, you might dread wearing it.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288001/best-sunscreens-for-rosacea-288001-1593649254035-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>When it comes to <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/how-to-prevent-rosacea\" target=\"_blank\">rosacea</a>, Cohen says the formulation type doesn't really affect the outcome, but there are some things to keep in mind when you're choosing a sunscreen, which he outlined below for us.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288001/best-sunscreens-for-rosacea-288001-1593649216802-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>Well, this is a guideline for everyone, but it's especially important for people with rosacea. \"Since inflammation is a cause and an outcome in rosacea, it is really important that the application of sunscreen every morning becomes a habit,\" Cohen says. \"Reducing the inflammation caused by UV exposure can really help to reduce flares in rosacea patients. And remember to reapply every two hours, or more frequently if sweating, swimming or toweling off.\"</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288001/best-sunscreens-for-rosacea-288001-1593649617662-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>\"It is important to avoid products with unnecessary synthetic fragrances as these can cause irritation,\" Cohen advises. The same goes for dyes, too.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288001/best-sunscreens-for-rosacea-288001-1593650100021-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>Cohen says that added antioxidants might be helpful for reducing inflammation and any damage caused by UV radiation.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288001/best-sunscreens-for-rosacea-288001-1593650171614-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>These are beneficial because they don't clog pores, Cohen says.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288001/best-sunscreens-for-rosacea-288001-1593649740081-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>\"Using a product that has a natural tint can be nice to minimize any facial redness you may be experiencing,\" Cohen suggests.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288001/best-sunscreens-for-rosacea-288001-1593649345716-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>Cohen says there are some sunscreens that have oils that are used to cover up the sunscreen smell. He advises against stocking up on those, as they can clog pores.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288001/best-sunscreens-for-rosacea-288001-1593649397676-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>Need more options for sunscreens? Take a look at some of Cohen's and our picks:</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288001/best-sunscreens-for-rosacea-288001-1593650349792-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Cohen recommends this tinted sunscreen to cover up any redness. It's noncomedogenic. It's also water-resistant and contains titanium dioxide and zinc oxide for broad-spectrum protection and CoEnzyme Q10 for antioxidant power.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288001/best-sunscreens-for-rosacea-288001-1593650662769-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Another rec from Cohen, this one from EltaMD is fragrance- and oil-free. Other ingredients include sodium hyaluronate to moisturize and lactic acid to clear pores.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288001/best-sunscreens-for-rosacea-288001-1593650891302-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>This mineral sunscreen is fast-absorbing and good for sensitive skin. It also contains antioxidants for free-radical protection.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288001/best-sunscreens-for-rosacea-288001-1593649500386-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288001/best-sunscreens-for-rosacea-288001-1593651296935-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Supergoop!'s Mattescreen is great because it's also as a primer and works to brighten and improve uneven skin tone, which can help with the redness from rosacea. It also contains butterfly bush extract, which provides protection against blue light from our screens.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288001/best-sunscreens-for-rosacea-288001-1593651386697-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>The antioxidant vitamin E in this sunscreen shields against free radicals while keeping the skin hydrated. here, primers are a very triggering category of <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/katie-jane-hughes-summer-makeup-skincare-tutorial\" target=\"_blank\">makeup</a> and <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/cassandra-grey-beauty-routine\" target=\"_blank\">skincare</a> within the beauty industry. I know plenty of makeup artists and fellow beauty editors who absolutely swear by them, and I know just as many who absolutely loathe them. For those who love them, primers are the ultimate way to ensure a smooth, oil- and budge-free makeup application. But for those who despise them, they're just a needless and often disappointing extra step in your routine. </p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/280855/best-drugstore-primers-280855-1561508006363-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>We won't tell you which camp to pitch a tent in, because honestly, whether or not you'll stan a makeup primer mainly comes down to personal preference <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/face-primers-for-dry-skin\" target=\"_blank\">regarding skin concerns</a>, the kind of finish you seek, the bandwidth of your beauty budget, and more. That said, if the only thing stopping you from experimenting or investing in a primer is a limited spending quota, we have great news: Some of the <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/best-primers-for-oily-skin\" target=\"_blank\">best primer formulas</a> in the business can be found at the drugstore or with drugstore-compatible prices. (Think mostly $20 and under!) </p><p>From primers for your lids to primers for your face and lips, all of our favorite drugstore beauty brands have come to our rescue, launching <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/best-primers-for-mature-skin\" target=\"_blank\">complexion-improving formulas</a> that you'll love if you're already camp primer and which might just convert you if you're not. Ahead, we're rolling out our 15 beloved primers found at three of our favorite drugstore-offering beauty retailers.
